Customer needs a specific breakdown of a Supper Menu, but was previously told of limitations in SchoolCafe where this would overwrite the Regular menus.

--- turn 1 [agent/private_note] agent:22038606503  2025-08-05T19:54:25Z ---
She has an 'At Risk Supper' (AKa After School Supper), she wants to assign Menus here but someone previously told her doing so would overwrite the 'Regular' menus, which I qualified with her to mean the reg. Brk, Lunch, etc. for the selected At Risk sites.  This didn't sound right, so we poked around on GTA and looked in a Guest view in SchoolCafe, I showed her the parent can see Brk, Lunch, Supper and Snack views separately - so do not believe this to be true.

However, this was complex enough - and she has used enough but this is tricky - that I suggested she book time with Yolissa for Q&A about this situation.  Since she's already been told different things (and since her FSD is already a little upset about ANOTHER limitation in Menus, different ticket) I thought having Yolissa look at this was appropriate.  She was fine with this solution.

Recap

The caller is experiencing difficulties assigning a cycle menu named 'K and K 12 breakfast 2526 new' to the calendar.

Kelley assisted the caller in troubleshooting the assignment issue, confirming the correct groups and settings.

The IT department performed a system rollover, and Kelley advised ensuring all computers are updated before the school year starts on the 21st.

--- turn 1 [agent/reply] "customercare@primeroedge.com" <customercare@primeroedge.com>  2025-08-13T17:01:32Z ---
Hello Jade,

It looks like you will need to change the Meal Type on the sites serving Supper from CACFP Supper to Supper.  This will allow you to assign the menu cycles as they are set up for Meal Type Supper:

Your menu cycle is for Super:

Once this is done, you can assign your CACFP Super menus  under Meal Type Supper

--- turn 1 [agent/reply] "customercare@primeroedge.com" <customercare@primeroedge.com>  2025-08-14T17:19:46Z ---
Hello Seon,

The reason some production records are showing up is that under the Rowlett high school on the days and menu lines that are showing up under Abbett elementary are showing that their is a food preparation site under the plans for site 009 Rowlett. You would need to update that on the production plans for Rowlett and it should fix the issues. That would explain why its sporadic and not everyday and different lines on different days. My guess is when Rowlett was doing their production plans they would have saved food preparation site under Abbett and it should be itself.  Let me know if you have any questions.

TICKET 294022  |  OL3 - Canutillo ISD - CACFP Supper
==========================================================================================

--- turn 0 [customer/description] Carla Chavira <cchavira@canutillo-isd.org>  2025-08-25T14:38:18Z ---
Carla called Chris Rios for assistance with the PrimeroEdge software. Chris guided Carla through correcting the meal type configuration and setting the default menu item, resolving the issues she was experiencing.

Recap

Carla contacted Chris because she was unable to post production records for high school supper menus in PrimeroEdge. She found that the high school option was missing when assigning menus under the supper meal type.

Chris identified that Carla was using the CACFP supper setting instead of the regular supper setting, which was causing the high school option to be unavailable. Carla corrected this in the program configuration.

Carla then noticed that the CACFP dinner high school menu item was not highlighted in red in her menu grid. Chris instructed her to open the CACFP dinner high school menu, go to the layout, and select CACFP dinner from the "no default menu item" dropdown, which resolved the highlighting issue.

--- turn 1 [agent/reply] "customercare@primeroedge.com" <customercare@primeroedge.com>  2025-08-27T17:35:40Z ---
Hello Arthur,

Good job on figuring out the "Assign Menus" process! That's HUGE!

To remove the menus - you'll go right back to that same page...

Menu Planning > Menus > Assign Menus

Make the selections at the top of page (you can even narrow it down to a specific site)

You will be able to click on the little trash bin on the top right hand corner of each date box, and it will remove that specific menu from ONLY the site that you select at the top. (That way if  you assigned it to a "group" of sites and only need to remove it from one, you have that ability.)

Let us know if you have any other questions.

customercare@primeroedge.com
 <
customercare@primeroedge.com
> wrote:

Hello Arthur,

Good job on figuring out the "Assign Menus" process! That's HUGE!

To remove the menus - you'll go right back to that same page...

Menu Planning > Menus > Assign Menus

Make the selections at the top of page (you can even narrow it down to a specific site)

You will be able to click on the little trash bin on the top right hand corner of each date box, and it will remove that specific menu from ONLY the site that you select at the top. (That way
 if  you assigned it to a "group" of sites and only need to remove it from one, you have that ability.)

Let us know if you have any other questions.

Recap

Chris Rios instructed the representative to go to menu planning, assign the snack menu to the relevant school, and select the appropriate meal type and start date for production.

TICKET 300340  |  WESTERN PA SCHOOL FOR DEAF - Assign menus after hours chat.
==========================================================================================

--- turn 0 [customer/description] Christi Beazley <christi@chgilbert.com>  2025-10-07T11:36:08Z ---
Christi Beazley




christi@chgilbert.com



05:11 AM, 07th Oct







Christi Beazley




I need to add K-8 menu line and 9-12 menu line. I went to configuration, menu lines and added K-8 and 9-12 for lunch however when going to assign menus, these lines are not showing, am I missing something?

Thank you for your help.



05:11 AM, 07th Oct







Keith




Hello, please try these steps:

Navigate to Site Configuration: Go to Menu Planning > Configuration > Site Configuration.

Select a Site: Find the site where you want to add the new lunch menu lines and click the arrow at the beginning of the row to expand the details.

Add or Edit the Meal Type:

Click Add Meal Type to Site.

Select "Lunch" as the Meal Type.

In the Menu Lines dropdown, select your newly created "K-8" and "9-12" menu lines.

Click Insert.

You will need to repeat these steps for each site where you want to use the new K-8 and 9-12 lunch menu lines. The system requires you to link Menu Lines to specific sites and meal types before they become available for menu assignment.



06:03 AM, 07th Oct

















Take to
Team Inbox

, Christi Beazley <christi@chgilbert.com> wrote:

How do I fix that?



Thank you for your time and help,

From:
 customercare@primeroedge.com <customercare@primeroedge.com>

Sent:
 Tuesday, October 7, 2025 7:37 AM

To:
 Christi Beazley <Christi@chgilbert.com>

Subject:
 Re: WESTERN PA SCHOOL FOR DEAF - Assign menus after hours chat.-[#300340]



Hello Christi,





Hello, please try these steps:



Navigate to Site Configuration: Go to Menu Planning > Configuration > Site Configuration.

Select a Site: Find the site where you want to add the new lunch menu lines and click the arrow at the beginning of the row to expand the details.

Add or Edit the Meal Type:

Click Add Meal Type to Site.

Select "Lunch" as the Meal Type.

In the Menu Lines dropdown, select your newly created "K-8" and "9-12" menu lines.

Click Insert.

You will need to repeat these steps for each site where you want to use the new K-8 and 9-12 lunch menu lines. The system requires you to link Menu Lines to specific sites and meal types before they become available for menu assignment.

--- turn 0 [customer/description] Jade Kelley <jade.kelley@smusd.org>  2025-10-08T16:59:09Z ---
Jade Kelley




Hi, if I add a quick list to menus that have already been assigned. Will this have any effect on planned productions?



11:17 AM, 08th Oct







Jade Kelley




I just need to add my quick list for daily fruit options



11:18 AM, 08th Oct







Keith




Adding a quick list for daily fruit options to menus that have already been assigned will not automatically affect the existing planned productions.



11:49 AM, 08th Oct

















Take to
Team Inbox

--- turn 1 [agent/reply] agent:22001856460  2025-10-08T16:59:15Z ---
Jade Kelley




Hi, did my question go through? It disappeared, but I sent it over 20 minutes ago



11:42 AM, 08th Oct







Keith




Adding a quick list for daily fruit options to menus that have already been assigned will not automatically affect the existing planned productions.



11:49 AM, 08th Oct







Keith




Production Plans: Production plans are generated based on the specific menu version that is assigned to that date. Therefore, until you replace the old menu with your new one on the calendar, the production plans will continue to reflect the original menu without your new fruit options.



11:50 AM, 08th Oct







Keith




To ensure your new daily fruit options appear in the planned productions, you will need to:

Add your quick list of fruit options to the desired menu.

Save this edited menu (which will be a new copy).

Go to Assign Menus and replace the previously assigned menu with your newly updated menu on the desired calendar dates.



11:50 AM, 08th Oct

















Take to
Team Inbox

--- turn 0 [customer/description] Jeri Walker <jeri.walker@gocommodores.org>  2025-10-16T16:07:55Z ---
Good morning. Is there a way to label a day on the menu as Manager's Choice? I use this instead of putting a menu right before holidays or on special occasions.

Thank you!

--

CONFIDENTIALITY NOTICE: This e-mail communication from the Lafayette County School District, including any attachments, is intended solely for the use of the designated recipient(s) named above and may contain confidential and privileged information. If you are not the intended recipient (or authorized to receive for the recipient), you are hereby notified that any review, disclosure, dissemination, distribution or copying of this communication is strictly prohibited.
This communication may contain material protected by the Family Educational Rights and Privacy Act (FERPA).
If you have received this communication in error, please contact the sender by reply e-mail and destroy all copies of this communication and any attachments.

--- turn 1 [agent/private_note] agent:22038606503  2025-10-16T19:25:19Z ---
It doesn't appear that there is a clean way to do this.  I bounced ideas off a Team Lead, thinking maybe an empty 'dummy' menu listing could be assigned, but then there are no serveable items assigned.  Also there are issues with Production (if they are using it).

Bottom line answer is there is no good way to accomplish this without creating much more work than just assigning a Menu normally.

--- turn 2 [agent/reply] "customercare@primeroedge.com" <customercare@primeroedge.com>  2025-10-16T19:42:48Z ---
Hello Jeri,

There is really no good way to do this.  I discussed with a Team Lead, thought possibly you could create a 'dummy' menu in Name only to Assign as a placeholder, but you would still have to swap in the 'actual' menu for that day before the serving day arrives to show the serving items.  Also, if you are using Production, this approach would create problems in that area of the system as well.

Consequently, we cannot advise doing this as it likely would create more work for you and could potentially incur the issues described above.

--- turn 9 [agent/private_note] agent:22003349747  2025-11-20T07:29:08Z ---
Hi Alekya,

This is not an issue on the SchoolCafe side. If you check the menus assigned to this school for lunch, there is a menu assigned for
20/11/2025
 that includes these categories.

These categories will also appear in the weekly view (for the week starting
17/11/2025
) and in the daily view for
20/11/2025
.

In the monthly view, we consolidate all categories configured throughout the month, which is why they are visible there as well. If they want to correct this, they will need to update the menus first and then republish them, which will resolve the issue.

TICKET 305108  |  Como-Pickton CISD - Copied Menu items not showing in Production
==========================================================================================

--- turn 0 [customer/description] JoAnn Fuller <fullerj@cpcisd.net>  2025-11-18T22:24:15Z ---
District called inquiring on a menu where they needed to change out the milk items and already copied the menu and added in the new ones but were not seeing the change reflect in Production

--- turn 1 [agent/private_note] agent:22034350878  2025-11-18T22:26:28Z ---
advised for copied menu you have to reassign. archive edit would replace the items. but archive and edit only shows up under certain circumstances (sale recorded).

she could reassign (step she hadn't done yet), but would need to re-enter counts. OR could add items under production direclty.

it won't delete the old but she can zero out the counts and post production analysis will not factor those in the count. It does go by the planned count.

TICKET 311852  |  Metz - Mount Laurel - Menu Assignment
==========================================================================================

--- turn 0 [customer/description] Laura D'Aiuto <mtl@nsfm.com>  2026-02-13T16:15:19Z ---
CAUTION
: This email originated from outside of the organization. Do not click links or open attachments unless you recognize the sender and know the content is safe.

Good morning,

I am having trouble posting my PreK menus. When I attempt to assign the menu, the "Menu Line" only provides the "regular" option. I want to ensure I do not override my Elementary menus during this process.

Could you please provide assistance with this? For reference, the buildings with PreK classes are:

- Hillside Elementary

- Fleetwood Elementary

- Parkway Elementary

Any support you can provide would be greatly appreciated, I look forward to hearing from you.

Best,

Laura D'Aiuto

Laura D'Aiuto

4 year Team Member

Food Service Director

NutriServe Food Management

                                  By Metz

Mount Laurel School District

ma1551@metzcorp.com

856-234-1610 ext. 22014

--- turn 1 [agent/reply] "customercare@primeroedge.com" <customercare@primeroedge.com>  2026-02-13T17:12:28Z ---
Hello Laura,

As the your PK group is also in the same site group Elementary as your K-8 and that your Menu is setup as K-8, I might recommend creating a second Menu Line where you can assign the menu for your PK students if you are using a separate menu. It looks like there is already a PreK menu line setup in your configuration, so you would just need to enable it under your site configuration for those schools.

Then when assigning you should be able to use the drop down for the 2nd menu line and when assigning it would only assign to those schools with that menu line.  This would not overwrite the Regular line.

Alternatively, some districts might use the same menu for both groups but perhaps with a different serving size and in this scenario could set the default serving size for PK on the items, then add PK group to existing menus under the regular line, etc.  However, I believe the first method may be the direction you are seeking.

Let us know if you have any questions regarding this ticket by replying all to this ticket

To the Primero Edge and Nutrislice Teams,

I am writing to formally express my escalating frustration with the ongoing integration issues between
Primero

Nutrislice
 that, as of today, are still not functioning 100% correctly.

This problem has been recurring since August (as previously noted by Lynn), and despite repeated discussions and troubleshooting efforts, we continue to experience the same failures.  We need clear accountability, definitive answers, and a resolution plan.

The current state of the integration is having a direct operational impact. It is forcing TNG team members to spend an excessive amount of time manually addressing issues that should be handled seamlessly by the API integration. Beyond the internal inefficiency, this is negatively affecting how TNG appears operationally, which is a serious concern.

What is most troubling is that this same Primero → Nutrislice API integration is reportedly functioning for other FSMC clients.  That raises significant questions about why our environment continues to experience persistent failures with no sustainable fix.

This situation cannot and will not continue in its current state.

I am requesting that we schedule a joint meeting (again) with both Primero and Nutrislice, along with Lynn Cesarini, as soon as possible to:

Identify the root cause (not assumptions)

Establish clear ownership of the issue(s)

Define a concrete resolution timeline

Confirm what is required to achieve a fully stable, reliable integration

We need alignment between both vendors and a unified path forward. I expect actionable answers and a commitment to resolution.

PrimeroEdge Team,

I hope everyone is doing well.

We are reaching out as we are seeing repeated issues where items marked as active in Primero Edge either do not show in the Enterprise level API responses, and/or the district level API responses. I know we have troubleshooted this with your team before,
 but we believe there may be a root cause here that needs to be further investigated.

From the Nutrislice perspective, we have not and are not actively seeing this with any other Nutrislice client using the PrimeroEdge integration, so we are curious as to where the disconnect is.

Please see below for examples.

Examples From This Week-

1)
 Tomato Bacon Grilled Cheese (
25/26 NGR110396)

This item is
not
 being returned to us with full detail
 from Primero Edge, so we can’t pull the detailed information into Nutrislice. In our joint ticket with Primero Edge in December (307965), PE indicated this happens when the item
 is not marked active under the
Recipe
 tab,
 but Lynn showed us it is in fact active.

2)
 Buffalo Chicken Quesadilla (110342), TNG Breakfast Griddle (NGR110379), Shamrock Pizza (NGR109407 / NGR109406)

These
 items are
only
 shared/synced down to districts if they exist in that district’s own Primero Edge database.
When we check the district codes TNG referenced (Port Allegany, Johnsonburg, etc.), based on what Nutrislice sees, these items
 do
not
 appear
 in those districts’ Primero Edge instances, which is why Nutrislice can’t show them for those districts.

3)
 General Tso Chicken w/ Mac & Cheese

We’re not finding this item anywhere in the
 Primero Edge data we’re receiving.

Historical Ticket Examples Mirroring the Same Behavior -

Ticket 265577 - Oct 31 2024

Ticket 303147 - Oct 31 2025

Ticket 307965 - December 23, 2025

Please let us know if tomorrow between 2-3 PM ET is available for the team to have a call.

All the best,

Grace

--- turn 8 [agent/private_note] agent:22004661029  2026-02-26T15:10:40Z ---
Select DS.Sourcename, R.RecipeCode, RD.RecipeName, R.StatusId RecipeStatus, RD.StatusId RecipeDetailStatus, MI.StatusId MenuItemStatus

from MP_Recipe R

JOIN MP_RecipeDetail RD ON R.RecipeId = RD.RecipeId

JOIN MP_MenuItem MI ON MI.RecipeId = R.RecipeId

JOIN MP_DataSource DS ON DS.DataSourceId = R.DataSourceId

WHERE (R.RecipeCode in ('NGR110396', '110342', 'NGR110379', 'NGR109406')

OR (RD.RecipeName like '%General%Tso%Chicken%Mac%Cheese%' OR RD.RecipeName like '%Buffalo%Chicken%Quesadilla%'))

PrimeroEdge Team,



I hope everyone is doing well.



We are reaching out as we are seeing repeated issues where items marked as active in Primero Edge either do not show in the Enterprise level API responses, and/or the district
 level API responses. I know we have troubleshooted this with your team before, but we believe there may be a root cause here that needs to be further investigated.



From the Nutrislice perspective, we have not and are not actively seeing this with any other Nutrislice client using the PrimeroEdge integration, so we are curious as to where
 the disconnect is.



Please see below for examples.



Examples From This Week-



1) Tomato Bacon Grilled Cheese (
25/26
 NGR110396)

This item is
not being returned to us with full detail
 from Primero Edge, so we can’t pull the
 detailed information into Nutrislice. In our joint ticket with Primero Edge in December (307965), PE indicated this happens when the item is not marked active under the
Recipe
 tab, but Lynn
 showed us it is in fact active.

2) Buffalo Chicken Quesadilla (110342), TNG Breakfast Griddle (NGR110379), Shamrock Pizza (NGR109407
 / NGR109406)

These items are only shared/synced down to districts if they exist in that district’s own Primero Edge database.
When
 we check the district codes TNG referenced (Port Allegany, Johnsonburg, etc.), based on what Nutrislice sees, these items do
not
 appear in those districts’ Primero Edge instances, which is why Nutrislice can’t show them for those districts.

3) General Tso Chicken w/ Mac & Cheese

We’re not finding this item anywhere in the Primero Edge data we’re receiving.

Hello Grace,

We identified an issue following a recent update to
PrimeroEdge
 (
v
1
5.17)
 that affected how menu item Tags were transmitted via the API to
Nutrislice
.
As a result, only menu items containing Tags were not syncing properly. All other menu items were unaffected.
A fix has been implemented and is currently being applied to the production environment. Once complete, we will validate the integration to ensure menu synchronization is functioning as expected.

Thank you for your patience as we resolve this matter.

Hello,

Thanks for the quick turnaround. We were able to sync the five example foods to the Enterprise org and can confirm:

Tomato Bacon Grilled Cheese
 is now appearing as expected.

General Tso’s Chicken

with Macaroni & Cheese
 has the updated name as expected.

Food Sharing:
  sharing in Nutrislice updates as each district syncs during the nightly process (which has just started). To validate today’s change, we manually ran a sync earlier for Port Allegany (Org ID: a8812cf0-8487-41dc-8ba0-290955e2741c)
 and confirmed additional foods that were missing earlier today are now present after that sync.

That said, we’re still seeing some differences between what’s available in the API and what TNG is expecting. Lynn mentioned that all

“NGR”
 items should be shared with all orgs. Earlier today, when we pulled an export from the TNG Enterprise org, we identified

20 NGR foods
 that were not shared with Port Allegany at that time. We also confirmed that, at that time, none of those 20 were being returned by the Foods API for that district.Port Allegany is just the example org we’ve been using to validate,
 but we expect the same pattern may be affecting other districts and potentially other items as well.

As of this evening:

1 of the 20 is now being returned (and we confirmed it was shared via the Nutrislice sync).

19 are still not being returned in the Foods API for Port Allegany.

Those same 19 items are also not appearing in the Enterprise API responses

I’ve included the list of the 20 foods we identified earlier today; the one now working is highlighted in green.

  — per our earlier conversations, we kept foods with “25/26” in the name during the Nutrislice food
 library cleanup. All of these items include “25/26” in the name but are not being returned from PE.

PrimeroEdge Team,



I hope everyone is doing well.



We are reaching out as we are seeing repeated issues where items marked as active in Primero Edge either do not show in the Enterprise level API responses, and/or the district level API responses.
 I know we have troubleshooted this with your team before, but we believe there may be a root cause here that needs to be further investigated.



From the Nutrislice perspective, we have not and are not actively seeing this with any other Nutrislice client using the PrimeroEdge integration, so we are curious as to where the disconnect
 is.



Please see below for examples.



Examples From This Week-



1) Tomato Bacon Grilled Cheese (
25/26
 NGR110396)

This item is
not being returned to us with full detail
 from
 Primero Edge, so we can’t pull the detailed information into Nutrislice. In our joint ticket with Primero Edge in December (307965), PE indicated this happens when the item is not marked active under the
Recipe
 tab,
 but Lynn showed us it is in fact active.

2) Buffalo Chicken Quesadilla (110342), TNG Breakfast Griddle (NGR110379), Shamrock Pizza (NGR109407 / NGR109406)

These items are only shared/synced down to districts if they exist in that district’s own Primero Edge database.
When
 we check the district codes TNG referenced (Port Allegany, Johnsonburg, etc.), based on what Nutrislice sees, these items do
not
 appear in those districts’ Primero Edge instances, which is why Nutrislice can’t show them for those districts.

3) General Tso Chicken w/ Mac & Cheese

We’re not finding this item anywhere in the Primero Edge data we’re receiving.

Hello,



Thanks for the quick turnaround. We were able to sync the five example foods to the Enterprise org and can confirm:

Tomato Bacon Grilled Cheese
 is now appearing as expected.

General Tso’s Chicken

with Macaroni & Cheese
 has the updated name as expected.

Food Sharing:
  sharing in Nutrislice updates as each district syncs during the nightly process (which has just started). To validate today’s change, we manually ran a sync earlier for Port Allegany (Org ID: a8812cf0-8487-41dc-8ba0-290955e2741c)
 and confirmed additional foods that were missing earlier today are now present after that sync.

That said, we’re still seeing some differences between what’s available in the API and what TNG is expecting. Lynn mentioned that all

“NGR”
 items should be shared with all orgs. Earlier today, when we pulled an export from the TNG Enterprise org, we identified

20 NGR foods
 that were not shared with Port Allegany at that time. We also confirmed that, at that time, none of those 20 were being returned by the Foods API for that district.Port Allegany
 is just the example org we’ve been using to validate, but we expect the same pattern may be affecting other districts and potentially other items as well.

As of this evening:

1 of the 20 is now being returned (and we confirmed it was shared via the Nutrislice sync).

19 are still not being returned in the Foods API for Port Allegany.

Those same 19 items are also not appearing in the Enterprise API responses

Hello Grace,

We identified an issue following a recent update to
PrimeroEdge
 (v15.17)  that
 affected how menu item Tags were transmitted via the API to
Nutrislice
.  As a result, only menu
 items containing Tags were not syncing properly. All other menu items were unaffected.  A fix has been implemented and is currently being applied to the production environment. Once complete, we will validate the integration to ensure menu synchronization
 is functioning as expected.

Thank you for your patience as we resolve this matter.

25/26
 NGR110396)

not being returned to us with full detail
 from Primero Edge, so we can’t pull the

Recipe
 tab, but Lynn
 showed us it is in fact active.

2) Buffalo Chicken Quesadilla (110342), TNG Breakfast Griddle (NGR110379), Shamrock Pizza (NGR109407
 / NGR109406)

not

3) General Tso Chicken w/ Mac & Cheese

We identified an issue following a recent update to

 (v15.17)  that
 affected how menu item Tags were transmitted via the API to
Nutrislice
.  As a result, only menu
 items containing Tags were not syncing properly. All other menu items were unaffected.  A fix has been implemented and is currently being applied to the production environment. Once complete, we will validate the integration to ensure menu synchronization
 is functioning as expected.

Thank you for your patience as we resolve this matter.

PrimeroEdge Team,



I hope everyone is doing well.



We are reaching out as we are seeing repeated issues where items marked as active in Primero Edge either do not show in the Enterprise level API responses, and/or the district
 level API responses. I know we have troubleshooted this with your team before, but we believe there may be a root cause here that needs to be further investigated.



From the Nutrislice perspective, we have not and are not actively seeing this with any other Nutrislice client using the PrimeroEdge integration, so we are curious as to where
 the disconnect is.



Please see below for examples.



Examples From This Week-



1) Tomato Bacon Grilled Cheese (
25/26
 NGR110396)

This item is
not being returned to us with full detail
 from
 Primero Edge, so we can’t pull the detailed information into Nutrislice. In our joint ticket with Primero Edge in December (307965), PE indicated this happens when the item is not marked active under the
Recipe
 tab,
 but Lynn showed us it is in fact active.

2) Buffalo Chicken Quesadilla (110342), TNG Breakfast Griddle (NGR110379), Shamrock Pizza
 (NGR109407 / NGR109406)

These items are only shared/synced down to districts if they exist
 in that district’s own Primero Edge database.
When we check the district codes TNG referenced (Port Allegany,
 Johnsonburg, etc.), based on what Nutrislice sees, these items do
not
 appear in those districts’ Primero Edge instances, which is why Nutrislice can’t show them for those districts.

3) General Tso Chicken w/ Mac & Cheese

We’re not finding this item anywhere in the Primero Edge data we’re receiving.

Historical Ticket Examples Mirroring the Same Behavior -

Ticket 265577 - Oct 31 2024

Ticket 303147 - Oct 31 2025

Ticket 307965 - December 23, 2025



Please let us know if tomorrow between 2-3 PM ET is available for the team to have a call.



All the best,

Grace

Hello Heidi,

The information in Production indicates the plans were added today at 10:36am
(reference incomplete production plan and one in withdrawal that shows added today then withdrawn at 2:07pm)

If you look at this week, you can see how it references it was added 1/20 at 8:01am then modified today
 (10:46am)

It does look like a non-operating day was put in place for that week at most schools (except highland elementary). Was highland elementary supposed to be open?

Even though a non-operating day when Assigning menus there are also some options as well that would affect whether it would still assign a menu during the week at sites even when a holiday or non-operating day, which seems to have occurred here.  If the "Skip Holidays" was unchecked it would still assign at all sites.

Under Menu planning it is not showing the trashcan for the holiday week as 3 sites (Dogwood and ValleyRanch for the whole week, Porter Elementary just for 2/16), did withdraw those records. If that is undone at those sites for this week it will then allow you to delete the menu assignment.

PM Christina Gifford <
Christina.Gifford@cybersoft.net
> wrote:

Hi Naomi,



Thank you for getting back to me!

Once you have your menus assigned to the calendar, it is fairly simple to publish them to the SchoolCafe Family Portal.

I will provide the steps below…

Click Menu Planning

Click Menus

Click Publish Menus

Change the start date, and how many days you want to publish

Click Find Assigned Menus

Publish These Menus



Hope this helps! If you still need assistance, you can utilize the Resource Tab and type in Publish Menus – it will take you step by step.



Please reach out at any time if there is anything else you need!

#313547

raised by Naomi Shadwell (naomi.shadwell@smusd.org).

Hi Praveen,

The district reported that they are unable to Publish the menus for their district. So, below is what I have verified.

1. Verified that Publish menus is working on all other district on this OL4 environment except for this District. So eliminated the possibility of the Publish menus API connectivity.

2. Verified All the system settings related to Menu Publishing, and nothing unusual.

3. Verified the Menu Lines are All set to Include when Publishing to SchoolCafe = YES.

4. The Setting was set to "Menu Calendar Assignment" for publishing.

5. They had menus assigned for the whole month of March.

6. Verified Publishing for 31 days at a time, It failed.

7.
Verified Publishing for 1 day at a time, It failed every day in February and March.

8. When looking up on SchoolCafé to see if there are any past menus Published, it shows NO Menus are Published.

9. Verified all MNP_ tables for data for the ISDId of this district and all tables were empty.

10. Have performed a Trace and on PrimeroEdge the Menus are being Published without any errors. But the response of Publish is coming as error, and data is not going to Schoolcafe.

11. Verified Event Viewer and Error Log tables on both PrimeroEdge and Schoolcafe and found nothing related to this issue reported here.

Trace on Primeroedge: The below SP is giving results on Primeroedge without any Errors for all the dates that I have tested for.

exec MP_MenuCalendar_GetMenuSummary @StartDate='2026-03-05 00:00:00',@EndDate='2026-03-05 00:00:00',@RegionId=35

--- turn 6 [agent/private_note] agent:22004661029  2026-03-05T22:04:53Z ---
Data that I have verified in Schoolcafe.

Select * from ISD Where ISDName like 'san marc%'

declare @isdid int = 4574

declare @datatransfermasterid int

select @datatransfermasterid = DataTransferISDMasterId from ISD where ISDId=@isdid

drop table  IF EXISTS #publishedmenus

drop table  IF EXISTS #publishedmenuitems

drop table  IF EXISTS #publishedmenudetail

drop table  IF EXISTS #publishedmenurdagroupids



SELECT DISTINCT MenuId INTO #publishedmenus

FROM dbo.MNP_MenuCalendarDetail MCD

join School s on s.SchoolId = MCD.SchoolId

where S.ISDId=@isdid and MCD.DataTransferISDMasterId=@datatransfermasterid

--select * from #publishedmenus

SELECT DISTINCT MD.MenuItemId INTO #publishedmenuitems

FROM dbo.MNP_MenuDetail MD

JOIN #publishedmenus DM ON DM.MenuId = MD.MenuId

where MD.DataTransferISDMasterId=@datatransfermasterid

--select * from #publishedmenuitems

SELECT MenuDetailId INTO #publishedmenudetail FROM dbo.MNP_MenuDetail WHERE MenuId IN (SELECT MenuId FROM #publishedmenus) and DataTransferISDMasterId=@datatransfermasterid

Select * from MNP_TrayXMenuItem where MenuItemId in ( select MenuItemId from #publishedmenuitems)

select * FROM dbo.MNP_MenuDetailRDAGroup WHERE MenuDetailId IN (SELECT MenuDetailId FROM #publishedmenudetail) and DataTransferISDMasterId=@datatransfermasterid

select * FROM dbo.MNP_MenuDetail WHERE MenuId IN (SELECT MenuId FROM #publishedmenus) and DataTransferISDMasterId=@datatransfermasterid

Select * from MNP_MenuItemMealContribution where MenuItemId in ( select MenuItemId from #publishedmenuitems)

select * from MNP_MenuItem where MenuItemId in ( select MenuItemId from #publishedmenuitems) and DataTransferISDMasterId= @datatransfermasterid

SELECT MenuRDAGroupId INTO #publishedmenurdagroupids FROM dbo.MNP_MenuRDAGroup WHERE MenuId IN (SELECT MenuId FROM #publishedmenus) and DataTransferISDMasterId=@datatransfermasterid

select * FROM dbo.MNP_MenuRDAGroupDetail WHERE MenuRDAGroupId IN (SELECT MenuRDAGroupId FROM #publishedmenurdagroupids)

select * FROM dbo.MNP_MenuRDAGroup WHERE MenuRDAGroupId IN (SELECT MenuRDAGroupId FROM #publishedmenurdagroupids) and DataTransferISDMasterId=@datatransfermasterid

select * FROM dbo.MNP_MenuCalendarDetail WHERE MenuId in (SELECT MenuId from #publishedmenus) and DataTransferISDMasterId=@datatransfermasterid

select * FROM dbo.MNP_Menu WHERE MenuId IN (SELECT MenuId FROM #publishedmenus) and DataTransferISDMasterId=@datatransfermasterid

Select * from MNP_Holiday_School where SchoolId in (Select SchoolId from School where ISDId=@isdid)

select * FROM dbo.MNP_Holiday WHERE DistrictId=@isdid

select * from MNP_GradeOrder where ISDId=@isdid and DataTransferISDMasterId=@datatransfermasterid

select * from MNP_MenuServingLines where ISDId=@isdid and DataTransferISDMasterId=@datatransfermasterid

Select * from MNP_MenuItemsServedTogether where DataTransferISDMasterId=@datatransfermasterid

GO

Change the start date, and how many days you want to publish

Click Find Assigned Menus


Publish These Menus




Hope this helps! If you still need assistance, you can utilize the Resource Tab and type in Publish Menus – it will take you step by step.



Please reach out at any time if there is anything else you need!

--- turn 22 [agent/reply] "customercare@primeroedge.com" <customercare@primeroedge.com>  2026-03-13T14:43:23Z ---
Hello Naomi,

Do you mean how you publish the updates using publish menus?

Navigate to Menu Planning -> Menus -> Publish Menus-> Select the Start date and Number of days to Publish -> Click on Fine Menus -> Then push Publish menus button.

Its the same normal publish menus function, but when ever you select the dates to publish for, it will detect all the updates or modifications happened for he date or dates selected, and publish the current data to SchoolCafé.

We are looking at our menu in SchoolCafe and noticed that some of the items have pictures when we view the menu as the Daily option. The images are uploaded to the recipes and then it shows up in SchoolCafe.

Is there a place where we can add alt-text to the images or do we need to do it on our end before uploading to PrimeroEdge? And will the alt-text transfer over to SchoolCafe once uploaded to PrimeroEdge?

--- turn 1 [agent/reply] "customercare@primeroedge.com" <customercare@primeroedge.com>  2026-03-26T16:26:16Z ---
Hello Kou,

Yes, alt-text would need to be added to the image before being uploaded and saved in Primero. Menus would then need to be republished after for image to update in schoolcafe.

--- turn 10 [agent/reply] "customercare@primeroedge.com" <customercare@primeroedge.com>  2026-05-20T17:48:14Z ---
Hello Kou,

Thank you for checking in with us and bringing this to our attention! SchoolCafé was indeed already WCAG level A compliant but has had to implement some new updates to properly handle newer screen readers to maintain (and improve) that level, which we implemented late last year. However, the alt-text does seem to be a gap. As for the ingredients list, it is possible that the reading was affected by a recent change to recursively-display a list in cases where sub-ingredients are also recipes with their own sub-ingredients.

We will escalate this to meet the new revised deadline of April 2027 (for districts your size) and keep you posted. However, to reduce subsequent tickets, please let us know here if you find any other irregularities so that we can add them to your the list and verify maximum coverage.

Thank you!

Please take a look at ticket

#315592

raised by USA PrimeroEdge Food Systems Support (primeroedgefoodsystemssupport.usa@sodexo.com).

Hi All,

The district has question regarding the Color coding used on the Menu items with "Exceeding Sugar Usage" vs the Menu Item with "Discontinued Ingredients".

The question and/ or concern is that, the RED color that is being used in both the above conditions seems to be a little different. So they want to know below:

1. Was is intentional to use 2 different shared of RED for Menu items with "Exceeding Sugar Usage" vs the Menu Item with "Discontinued Ingredients".

2. If this was intentional then the color for when exceeding sugar content is currently more difficult for their users to identify in the system.

3.  They would like us to further look into making all of the shades match so that it is easier for users to see on screen.

4. They also have submitted another request to change the FONT for the Items being indicated with RED so the people that are color blinded can recognize the items. ref ticket :
https://primeroedge.freshdesk.com/a/tickets/315591

--- turn 9 [agent/reply] "customercare@primeroedge.com" <customercare@primeroedge.com>  2026-04-01T14:06:14Z ---
Hello Sodexo Team,

We do have the multiple red tones on these items. It was determined that a difference would be appropriate as the decision to serve or not serve the menu items that were not sugar-compliant is at the discretion of the menu planner or nutritionist at a district, and may not be something that should be considered as much of an "alert" status to sites. The brighter red is the one that sites should likely be trained to notify their management about, as there may be a problem with getting/using the no longer active ingredients.

The non-sugar-compliant items are a choice that some districts may leave on their menus, particularly their ala carte menus, as they've made the determination that some form of breakfast is better than no breakfast... but that the students will need to pay for those ala carte items and not include them in a meal. Since many districts use a particular menu line to handle their ala carte menus for the ease of ordering and withdrawals, this difference in their training process is a relevant necessity.

It is a discussion I can broach with districts at a future time to poll for options, but I don't anticipate an immediate change to these font effects.

PrimeroEdge

Hello Sodexo Team,

We do have the multiple red tones on these items. It was determined that a difference would be appropriate as the decision to serve or not serve the menu items that were not sugar-compliant is at the discretion of the menu planner or nutritionist at a district,
 and may not be something that should be considered as much of an "alert" status to sites. The brighter red is the one that sites should likely be trained to notify their management about, as there may be a problem with getting/using the no longer active ingredients.

The non-sugar-compliant items are a choice that some districts may leave on their menus, particularly their ala carte menus, as they've made the determination that some form of breakfast is better than no breakfast... but that the students will need to pay
 for those ala carte items and not include them in a meal. Since many districts use a particular menu line to handle their ala carte menus for the ease of ordering and withdrawals, this difference in their training process is a relevant necessity.

It is a discussion I can broach with districts at a future time to poll for options, but I don't anticipate an immediate change to these font effects.

--- turn 3 [agent/private_note] agent:22039013083  2026-03-31T22:13:58Z ---
The answer here is multi faceted. For starters I will go from the 2 screenshots above:

- The cycle she created is for Meal Type Breakfast, but when trying to search they are looking for Meal type Summer Breakfast

That is the answer right there, but it does get a little deeper. For starters all of their cycles under that pattern are the same

- This is the least important bit, but when it comes to calculating data and nutritionals under a meal pattern, there are certain things that get factored in. This is where I would maybe clarify with them. The SFSP program they are trying to use calculates based on age, but in 99% of scenarios nutrition data should be pulled by grade, not age. People think summer and automatically assume they need to be making SFSP menus, but for a lot of people it is not needed. I don't know if this district needs it or not, but we can adjust once we find out.

Let me know if you have any questions

--- turn 4 [agent/private_note] agent:22044930030  2026-04-01T11:59:30Z ---

: This email originated from outside of the organization. Do not click links or open attachments unless you recognize the sender and know the content is safe.

Good morning,

During the summer, not all of our sites operate. Is there a way to assign menus to a specific elementary, middle school, or high school without including every site?

Meshala Huff

Email:
meshala.huff@paisd.org

CONFIDENTIALITY NOTICE:  This message from the Port Arthur Independent School District may contain confidential or privileged information. If you received this transmission in error,
 please return it to the sender and delete the material from any computer. Disclosure or use of any part of this message by persons other than the intended recipient is prohibited.

--- turn 1 [agent/reply] "customercare@primeroedge.com" <customercare@primeroedge.com>  2026-04-27T14:34:37Z ---
Hello Meshala,

You don't have to assign to everything at once.

In the Assign screen (see sample data screen below), choose to 'filter' by Meal Type, Site Group and Menu line, and then from the Organization Level drop down you would choose the unique Site you want to assign to and then Assign.

If you have several schools to do, simply repeat after choosing each specific school you want to Assign to.

--- turn 4 [agent/private_note] agent:22038606503  2026-04-28T14:35:41Z ---
I've asked both Terri and Richard for input on this ... Terri had no suggestions from Assign Menu POV, seeing what Richard might suggest.

Richards response:

Richard Benson

09:43 AM

I can't think of a way this would be possible. There would be too many complications from creating a generic non-site, adding licenses, configurations, adding serving groups, etc... Plus everyone would need to view menus as a guest in SchoolCafe rather than from their accounts. They would still need to select a site, grade and serving line.

--- turn 5 [agent/reply] "customercare@primeroedge.com" <customercare@primeroedge.com>  2026-04-28T16:53:26Z ---
Hello Amy,

I had never come across this type of request before, so asked for input from two Team Leads - both with many years of experience - for any ideas; unfortunately, since everything in PrimeroEdge is Site-based, t
hey felt there would be too many complications involved in creating a generic 'non-site', including adding licenses, configurations, adding serving groups, etc. to make this a workable option to pursue.

In addition, an added complication with that idea is that parents would need to view menus as a 'Guest' in SchoolCafe (rather than from their actual accounts), and even then they would still need to select a Site, Grade and Serving Line to view the Menus.

Hello Amy,

I had never come across this type of request before, so asked for input from two Team Leads - both with many years of experience - for any ideas; unfortunately, since everything in PrimeroEdge is Site-based, t
hey
 felt there would be too many complications involved in creating a generic 'non-site', including adding licenses, configurations, adding serving groups, etc. to make this a workable option to pursue.

In
 addition, an added complication with that idea is that parents would need to view menus as a 'Guest' in SchoolCafe (rather than from their actual accounts), and even then they would still need to select a Site, Grade and Serving Line to view the Menus.

--- turn 11 [agent/private_note] agent:22038606503  2026-04-29T19:44:38Z ---
Called Amy but we still couldn't get this sorted out.  Francesca took a look and said its because the Maple Grove ES is already assigned to 'Elementary School', and can't be part of 2 Site GROUPS at once.  She has named 'Summer Feeding' everywhere - Site Group, Menu Lines, etc - so its confusing; she can have multiple Menu Lines at a Site, but only one Site Group.

Will have to research and cb.  Amy doesn't want to mess up Production in place already, but wants to publish menus now for Summer.

--- turn 12 [agent/private_note] agent:22038606503  2026-04-29T19:56:25Z ---
Experimented in UAT for changing Site GROUPS - in SITE CONFIGURATION she CAN change to 'Summer Feeding' Site Group as of whatever Effective Date she puts in (becomes active the next day), BUT THIS WILL CLEAR PRODUCTION PLANS although she would be warned of it, as below:

She would have to wait until right before the change date, because changing now would remove Maple Grove as an Elementary Site, so any setups under 'Elementary' assumably would be roasted.  Then she would have to go through the same thing to flip back to regular Elementary group after Summer is over, with timing again being a critical consideration.

As Francesca had said, switching Site Groups really isn't feasible due to super-tricky timing.

--- turn 13 [agent/private_note] agent:22038606503  2026-04-30T14:29:45Z ---
Further testing in UTAT after talking to Terri .... this sequence should work:

she can add the 'Summer Feeding' menu LINE under existing 'Lunch' meal type in Maple Grove

she already has Summer Menus assigned to the Summer Feeding GROUP, so will need to copy these over to the Elementary GROUP

next she can (right now) assign these Summer menus to Maple Grove but under the Summer Feeding Menu LINE - she can use whatever start date she wants

Here is where I tested a way to avoid confusion for parents looking up current menus:

after assigning out all the Summer menus under Summer Feeding Menu Line, she can turn that Line back OFF (uncheck) for Lunch type at Maple Grove

this will 'Hide' the Summer Feeding Menu Line choice for parents, but will NOT remove the Assigned menus or the Production record entry based on my test

right before the date they start the summer meals, she can go back in and re-enable the Summer Feeding menu Line in Maple Grove (and turn OFF the regular Elem Lunch line too) to make it easy for SC parents to lookup these Summer Menus

I did not test as far as publishing, but she would need to publish at some point with Summer Feeding enabled to get the menus into SC.  She can choose whatever Start Date when she publishes as well as how many days to publish.

--- turn 14 [agent/reply] "customercare@primeroedge.com" <customercare@primeroedge.com>  2026-04-30T15:46:47Z ---
Hello Amy,

Since we last spoke, I've been testing to find a way to isolate the Summer Menus in your SchoolCafe view.

I discovered that, while it is technically possible to put Maple Grove under another Site GROUP, you cannot have more than one Site Group assigned to a school at a time.  This means if you switched from Elementary to Summer Feeding Site GROUP at a site, it would wipe out everything assigned to the Elementary GROUP, so this is not viable.

The only practical way I see to somewhat isolate summer Menus seen in SchoolCafe is to use multiple Menu LINES at that school.  I did some testing in your training database and believe the following sequence should work:

you can add the 'Summer Feeding' menu
LINE
 under existing 'Lunch' meal type in Maple Grove (we talked about this the other day, see below)

you already have Summer Menus assigned to the Summer Feeding GROUP; but you will need to copy these over to the Elementary GROUP to use them at Maple Grove.

once menus are copied, you can (right now) assign the Summer menus to Maple Grove
but under the Summer Feeding Menu LINE


With all that done, the following is an idea I tested and confirmed should work to avoid confusion for parents looking up current menus in SchoolCafe:

after assigning out all the Summer menus under Summer Feeding Menu
Line
, you can turn that Line back OFF (uncheck it) for the Lunch type at Maple Grove

this will 'Hide' the Summer Feeding Menu Line choice for parents, but will NOT remove the Assigned menus or the Production record entries added for summer - based on my tests they are still retained.

right before the date you start the summer meals, you can go back in and re-enable the Summer Feeding menu
Line
 in Maple Grove (and turn OFF the regular Elem Lunch line too) to make it easy for parents to lookup these Summer Menus in SchoolCafe.  You will again see the menus you Assigned under the Summer Feeding Line.

Lastly, you would need to publish - with Summer Feeding Menu Line enabled - to get the summer menus into SchoolCafe.  You can choose whatever Start Date desired when you publish as well as how many days to publish, so my thought is you could wait to do this until the day before Summer feeding starts.

I wanted to send this ahead of speaking with you about it so it makes more sense when we discuss.

Hello Amy,

Since we last spoke, I've been testing to find a way to isolate the Summer Menus in your SchoolCafe view.

 at a site, it would wipe out everything assigned to the Elementary GROUP, so this is not viable.

The only practical way I see to somewhat isolate summer Menus seen in SchoolCafe is to use multiple Menu LINES at that school.  I did some testing in your training database and believe the following sequence should work:

you can add the 'Summer Feeding' menu
LINE
 under existing 'Lunch' meal type in Maple Grove (we talked about this the other day, see below)

you already have Summer Menus assigned to the Summer Feeding GROUP; but you will need to copy these over to the Elementary GROUP to use them at Maple Grove.

once menus are copied, you can (right now) assign the Summer menus to Maple Grove

but under the Summer Feeding Menu LINE

Line

right before the date you start the summer meals, you can go back in and re-enable the Summer Feeding menu

Line
 in Maple Grove (and turn OFF the regular Elem Lunch line too) to make it easy for parents to lookup these Summer Menus in SchoolCafe.  You will again see the menus you Assigned under the Summer Feeding Line.

--- turn 3 [agent/reply] "customercare@primeroedge.com" <customercare@primeroedge.com>  2026-05-18T14:44:37Z ---
Hello Lauren,

In order to resume on Week 3 Day 1 after the Thanksgiving break, select Menu instead of Menu Cycle when clicking November 20th, 2026:

By clicking Menu instead of Menu Cycles, you can assign individual days within the menu cycle itself, and then choose 11/30/2026 and select specifically Lunch Menu SY 2027 (HS) W3 D1 to assign that day to the 30th, which will allow you to bypass the issue of assigning the menu cycle but having it resume on week 4 instead of 3 after the break:

Thank you,

In accordance with federal civil rights law and U.S. Department of Agriculture (USDA) civil rights regulations and policies, this institution is prohibited from discriminating on the basis
 of race, color, national origin, sex, disability, age, or reprisal or retaliation for prior civil rights activity.

Program information may be made available in languages other than English. Persons with disabilities who require alternative means of communication to obtain program information (e.g., Braille, large print, audiotape, American Sign Language), should contact
 the responsible state or local agency that administers the program or USDA’s TARGET Center at (202) 720-2600 (voice and TTY) or contact USDA through the Federal Relay Service at (800) 877-8339.

To file a program discrimination complaint, a Complainant should complete a Form AD-3027, USDA Program Discrimination Complaint Form which can be obtained online at:

https://www.usda.gov/sites/default/files/documents/ad-3027.pdf
,
 from any USDA office, by calling (866) 632-9992, or by writing a letter addressed to USDA. The letter must contain the complainant’s name, address, telephone number, and a written description of the alleged discriminatory action in sufficient detail to inform
 the Assistant Secretary for Civil Rights (ASCR) about the nature and date of an alleged civil rights violation. The completed AD-3027 form or letter must be submitted to USDA by:



1. Mail:

CAUTION
: This email originated from outside of the organization. Do not click links or open attachments unless you recognize the sender and know the content is safe.

I figured it out. When I hovered over the calendar, it showed that a holiday had been assigned. After checking the 2026–2027 school year holiday schedule, I found that a Thanksgiving holiday had mistakenly been applied to all of July and August, which was blocking
 those dates. I removed the holiday, and the calendar returned to normal (white), allowing us to assign menus successfully.

==========================================================================================
TICKET 320292  |  Springdale Schools - Confirmation on Adding Summer Breakfast and Lunch menus to relevant sites
==========================================================================================

--- turn 0 [customer/description] Tina Nodine <tina.nodine@sdale.org>  2026-05-18T16:50:20Z ---
Tina reached out reporting an issue of some sites not having the assigned summer breakfast lines after she assigned menus from the district organizational level and site/meal type. Investigated it further and found not all relevant sites have line 1 and 2 offered hence some of them lacking it, advised she go to the handful of sites who will do summer feeding and just individually assign them as there's not much uniformity for the district between their use of Line 2 for the school year vs line 2 solely for summer feeding program, and applying the summer menus at the organizational level will assign it to many sites not doing summer feeding.

--- turn 1 [agent/reply] "customercare@primeroedge.com" <customercare@primeroedge.com>  2026-05-18T16:52:07Z ---
Hello Tina,

It was a pleasure speaking to you today.

As mentioned before, creating new menu lines catered to summer breakfast and summer lunch would fix the issue of assigning the summer menus from the district organizational level not applying to some sites it should be, and applying to others it's not applicable to as you could solely select the menu line in question.

If not, just check the individual sites in the assign menu view to see if their breakfast and lunch are configured per their program requirements.

Thank you,
